class=\"TEXT_w_Indent\">Brussels • The latest developments involving Greece and its bailout negotiations:</p>\n<p class=\"TEXT_w_Indent\">———</p>\n<p class=\"TEXT_w_Indent\">8:50 a.m. MDT</p>\n<p class=\"TEXT_w_Indent\">Finnish Finance Ministrer Alexander Stubb says that the eurozone meeting on Greece has wrapped for the day without an agreement on new bailout loans for the country.</p>\n<p class=\"TEXT_w_Indent\">Stubb wrote on his official Twitter account: \"Eurogroup back later, but not today.\"</p>\n<p class=\"TEXT_w_Indent\">The decision is a big setback since there had been hopes to wrap up the bailout negotiations in time for European leaders to approve a deal later in the day.</p>\n<p class=\"TEXT_w_Indent\">Greece needs new loans by June 30, when it has a debt repayment it content-area content-full-article pull-right\">\n\n\t\t\t<div class=\"p402_premium\"> <!-- googlesurvey -->\n\n\t\t<div class=\"article\">\n\n\t\t<!--STORYBODY-->\n\t\t\t<p class=\"TEXT_w_Indent\">———</p>\n<p class=\"TEXT_w_Indent\">8:45 a.m. MDT</p>\n<p class=\"TEXT_w_Indent\">The International Monetary Fund says Greece will not get any extra time to make a debt repayment it owes the organization on June 30.</p>\n<p class=\"TEXT_w_Indent\">Greece owes the IMF 1.6 billion euros on June 30 but does not have the money to pay it. It is in talks with creditors, including the IMF, on getting more loans before then.</p>\n<p class=\"TEXT_w_Indent\">IMF spokesman Gerry Rice says \"We're expecting the payment to be made June 30,\" adding that Greece will be granted no extensions.</p>\n<p class=\"TEXT_w_Indent\">He says creditors are \"on the same page\" about the need for Athens to introduce deeper reforms. The creditors say a Greek proposal this week didn't go far enough and needs to make deeper cuts in the costly pension system, while sparing the poor.</p>\n<p class=\"TEXT_w_Indent\">Despite the impasse in talks, the IMF says it would be flexible. \"The IMF doesn't do take it or leave it,\" Rice said. \"That's not how we work. It's always give and take.\"</p>\n<p class=\"TEXT_w_Indent\">———</p>\n<p class=\"TEXT_w_Indent\">8:15 a.m. MDT</p>\n<p class=\"TEXT_w_Indent\">French President Francois Hollande is exhorting Greece and its international creditors to speed up talks on new loans for the country, as a default would affect the entire continent.</p>\n<p class=\"TEXT_w_Indent\">With decisive talks between dragging on for days, Hollande says that \"when Greece, Europe, the eurozone is at stake, we have to know how to finish negotiations.\"\n\t\t\t</p><div class=\"hidden-xs hidden-sm\">\n\t\t\t  <hr
